The app also comes with several tone mapping algorithms that converts HDR image back to SDR image. \r\n\r\nIf you are wondering how the magic happens behind the screen, here is a good explanation: https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=bkQJdaGGVM8\r\n\r\nYou can use this app to develop raw files.
